# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Current Feedback op amps:
 ^D6G4bxaj

Non-inverting ^Nej6WItx

z=Vout/Iin

Z x I1 = Z x Iin
    = Vout/Iin x Iin
    = Vout 

Vti = I2(Zf + Zg//Zb) -> 1

current Divider
    I1 = Zg/(Zg+Zb) x I2
    I2 = I1 x (Zg+Zb)/Zg ->2
    I1=Vout/z ->3

From 1 & 2
Vti = I1 x [(Zg+Zb)/Zg][(Zf + Zg//Zb)]
Add I1 from 3
Vti = (Vout/z)x [(Zg+Zb)/Zg][(Zf + Zg//Zb)]

Vout/Vti = z/(Zf(1+ Zb/[Zf//Zg]))

 ^iGVCAw3r

Inverting ^9TSWlvSH

I1= I+I2

I + (Vin - Va)/Zg = (Va-Vout)/Zf -> 1
    -Va = IZb -> 2
Vout =I2 ->3

Vout/Vin = {Z/[Zg(1+Zb/ZF//Zg)]}/{1+ [Z/[Zg(1+Zb/ZF//Zg)]]}
 ^NOQi6hIu

- Eqn for vout & vin for inverting and non inverting anaylsis ^YpT0QImp

Stability Analysis ^HhgT9YUS

- Rf define stability of the amplifier
- It is important to select Rf properly
- Rf value range given by the manufacturer
- If different value to be used, results of loop gain are extrapolated assuming linear relation ^AqsxZLOO

Zin = ZF1 + Zb((1+(Zf1/Zg1) - (1+Zfn/Zgn)) ^uM6g4TRD

Second Method: We can use graphical method to select Rf value 
For a given gain, calculate Rf & from Rf calculate Bandwidth of the amplifier ^L3gCIO7y

Stray capacitance gets introduced across input resistor, Hence Zd becomes reactive
Zg=Rg/1+RgCgs

Ab = Z/Zb + Zf/(Zg^2 + ZbZg)
Zb=Rb; Zg=Rg

From 1 & 2 loop gain is given by:
Ab= Z/(Rf(1+Rb/Rf//Rg)(1+Rn//Rf//RgCgs)

Loop gain is added with one pole. ^Fst65Z7a

Rf ^noEXj3bg

Cg ^T1yZCmUb

Rg ^0ZpfpLRF

Rf ^cfN6oqMW

Cg ^pR5obzQs

Rg ^CCQGVvFs

Cf ^Io6Qa1Sq

This above ckt wont change the number of poles n zeros
phase margin is worse with 3 poles, 2 is somewhat ideal. ^H2l77fN2

LVDS- Low voltage differential signal ^XKMkXBCP

This uses output in the form of differential output from fully differential op amps ^RYcDUo2i

Fully Differential Op Amp ^VQGuoNWD

- Increased immunity to external noise
- Increased output voltage swing for a given voltage
 ^vuvbgl3l

Using KCL & KVL
(Vin-V1)/Rg = (V1-Vout)/Rf

(Vin/Rg)-(Vl/Rg) = V1/Rf - (Vout+/Rf)

V1/Rf+V1/Rg = (Vin-/Rg) + (Vout/Rf)

V1= (Vin-/Rg + Vout+/Rf)(RfRg/Rf+Rg)

For V2:

(Vin+  - V2)/Rg = (V2 - Vout-)/Rf

V2(1/Rg + 1/Rf)= (Vin+/Rg) + (Vout-/Rf)

V2= (Vin+/Rg + Vout-/Rf)(RfRg/Rf+Rg)

V1=V2

(Vin-/Rg + Vout+/Rf)(RfRg/Rf+Rg)= (Vin+/Rg + Vout-/Rf)(RfRg/Rf+Rg)

(Vin-/Rg) +( Vout+/Rf) = (Vin+/Rg) + (Vout-/Rf)

(Vout+ - Vout-)/(Vin+ - Vin-)  =Rf/Rg
 ^KUTlKoEN
